        <a href="{{ section.settings.link_5_url | default: '#contact' }}" class="jz-mobile-nav-link">
          <svg width="20" height="20" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2">

            <polyline points="22,6 12,13 2,6"/>

  {%- comment -%} Mobile Menu Overlay {%- endcomment -%}
  <div class="jz-mobile-overlay" id="jzMobileOverlay" onclick="window.jzCloseMobileMenu && window.jzCloseMobileMenu(event); return false;"></div>


</header>


<script>
  // ULTRA SIMPLE GLOBAL FUNCTIONS - Works immediately
  window.jzOpenMobileMenu = function(e) {
    try {
      if (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        e.stopPropagation();
      }
      
      var menu = document.getElementById('jzMobileMenu');
      var overlay = document.getElementById('jzMobileOverlay');
      
      if (menu) menu.classList.add('jz-active');
      if (overlay) overlay.classList.add('jz-active');
      
      document.body.style.overflow = 'hidden';
      
      return false;
    } catch(err) {
      console.error('Menu error:', err);
      return false;
    }
  };
  
  window.jzCloseMobileMenu = function(e) {
    try {
      if (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        e.stopPropagation();
      }
      
      var menu = document.getElementById('jzMobileMenu');
      var overlay = document.getElementById('jzMobileOverlay');
      
      if (menu) menu.classList.remove('jz-active');
      if (overlay) overlay.classList.remove('jz-active');
      
      document.body.style.overflow = '';
      
      return false;
    } catch(err) {
      console.error('Close menu error:', err);
      return false;
    }
  };
  
  // Make functions available immediately
  console.log('Mobile menu functions loaded');

  (function() {
    // Wait for DOM to be ready
    function initNavigation() {
      // Elements
      const header = document.getElementById('jzHeader') || document.querySelector('.jz-header-section');
      const mobileMenu = document.getElementById('jzMobileMenu');
      const mobileOverlay = document.getElementById('jzMobileOverlay');
      const mobileMenuToggle = document.getElementById('jzMobileToggle');
      const mobileMenuClose = document.getElementById('jzMobileMenuClose');

      // Remove preload class slightly later to enable transitions
      if (header) {
        setTimeout(() => {
          header.classList.remove('jz-preload');
        }, 100);
      }

    // Helper to show hidden elements
    function showElement(el) {
      if (!el) return;
      // 1. Remove the strict inline hiding style
      el.style.display = 'flex'; // or block based on element
      el.style.visibility = 'visible';
      el.style.opacity = '1';
      
      // 2. Force reflow to enable transition
      void el.offsetWidth;
      
      // 3. Add active class for transition
      el.classList.add('jz-active');
    }

    // Helper to hide elements with transition
    function hideElement(el) {
      if (!el) return;
      // 1. Remove active class to start transition out
      el.classList.remove('jz-active');
      
      // 2. Wait for transition to finish before applying display: none
      setTimeout(() => {
        if (!el.classList.contains('jz-active')) {
          // Re-apply strict hiding styles
          if (el.id === 'jzMobileMenu') {
            el.style.cssText = 'display: none !important; visibility: hidden !important; opacity: 0 !important; transform: translate3d(-100%, 0, 0) !important;';
          } else {
            el.style.cssText = 'display: none !important; visibility: hidden !important; opacity: 0 !important;';
          }
        }
      }, 400); // Match CSS transition duration
    }



    // Mobile Menu Logic
    function openMobileMenu(e) {
      if (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        e.stopPropagation();
      }
      
      if (!mobileMenu || !mobileOverlay) {
        console.error('Mobile menu elements not found');
        return;
      }
      
      // Remove any inline styles that might block
      mobileMenu.removeAttribute('style');
      mobileOverlay.removeAttribute('style');
      
      // Show overlay first
      mobileOverlay.style.cssText = 'display: block !important; visibility: visible !important; opacity: 0 !important;';
      void mobileOverlay.offsetWidth; // Force reflow
      
      // Show menu - set base styles
      mobileMenu.style.cssText = 'display: flex !important; visibility: visible !important; opacity: 0 !important; transform: translate3d(-100%, 0, 0) !important;';
      void mobileMenu.offsetWidth; // Force reflow
      
      // Add active class with slight delay to trigger transition
      requestAnimationFrame(() => {
        mobileOverlay.classList.add('jz-active');
        mobileMenu.classList.add('jz-active');
      });
      
      // Prevent body scroll
      const scrollY = window.scrollY;
      document.body.style.cssText = `overflow: hidden !important; position: fixed !important; width: 100% !important; top: -${scrollY}px !important;`;
      
      // Store scroll position for restoration
      document.body.dataset.scrollY = scrollY;
    }

    function closeMobileMenu(e) {
      if (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        e.stopPropagation();
      }
      
      if (!mobileMenu || !mobileOverlay) return;
      
      // Remove active classes to trigger transition out
      mobileMenu.classList.remove('jz-active');
      mobileOverlay.classList.remove('jz-active');
      
      // Wait for transition to finish, then hide
      setTimeout(() => {
        if (!mobileMenu.classList.contains('jz-active')) {
          mobileMenu.style.cssText = 'display: none !important; visibility: hidden !important; opacity: 0 !important; transform: translate3d(-100%, 0, 0) !important;';
          mobileOverlay.style.cssText = 'display: none !important; visibility: hidden !important; opacity: 0 !important;';
        }
      }, 400); // Match CSS transition duration
      
      // Restore body scroll
      const scrollY = document.body.dataset.scrollY || 0;
      document.body.removeAttribute('style');
      document.body.removeAttribute('data-scroll-y');
      window.scrollTo(0, parseInt(scrollY) || 0);
    }

    // Mobile menu - Use global functions via onclick in HTML, but also add event listeners as backup
    if (mobileMenuToggle) {
      mobileMenuToggle.style.pointerEvents = 'auto';
      mobileMenuToggle.style.cursor = 'pointer';
      
      // Backup event listeners
      mobileMenuToggle.addEventListener('click', window.jzOpenMobileMenu, true);
      mobileMenuToggle.addEventListener('touchstart', function(e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        window.jzOpenMobileMenu(e);
      }, { passive: false, capture: true });
    }
    
    if (mobileMenuClose) {
      mobileMenuClose.onclick = window.jzCloseMobileMenu;
      mobileMenuClose.addEventListener('click', window.jzCloseMobileMenu);
      mobileMenuClose.addEventListener('touchstart', function(e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        window.jzCloseMobileMenu(e);
      }, { passive: false });
    }
    
    if (mobileOverlay) {
      mobileOverlay.onclick = window.jzCloseMobileMenu;
      mobileOverlay.addEventListener('click', window.jzCloseMobileMenu);
      mobileOverlay.addEventListener('touchstart', function(e) {
        if (e.target === mobileOverlay) {
          e.preventDefault();
          window.jzCloseMobileMenu(e);
        }
      }, { passive: false });
    }
    
    // Close on ESC key
    document.addEventListener('keydown', function(e) {
      if (e.key === 'Escape' && mobileMenu && mobileMenu.classList.contains('jz-active')) {
        window.jzCloseMobileMenu();
      }
    });


    // Close mobile menu immediately when clicking any link, then scroll
    const mobileNavLinks = document.querySelectorAll('.jz-mobile-nav-link');
    mobileNavLinks.forEach(link => {
      link.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
        const href = this.getAttribute('href');
        
        // If it's an anchor link
        if (href && href.startsWith('#') && href !== '#') {
          e.preventDefault();
          e.stopPropagation();
          
          // Close menu immediately first
          window.jzCloseMobileMenu();
          
          // Restore body scroll immediately
          document.body.style.overflow = '';
          document.body.style.position = '';
          document.body.style.width = '';
          
          // Small delay for menu to close, then scroll
          setTimeout(function() {
            scrollToAnchor(href);
            history.pushState(null, null, href);
          }, 100);
        } else {
          // For regular links, just close menu
          window.jzCloseMobileMenu();
        }
      }, true); // Use capture to execute before other handlers
    });
    

    // Close mobile menu on window resize to desktop size
    let resizeTimer;
    window.addEventListener('resize', function() {
      clearTimeout(resizeTimer);
      resizeTimer = setTimeout(function() {
        if (window.innerWidth > 768) {
          // Close immediately without animation on resize
          if (mobileMenu && mobileMenu.classList.contains('jz-active')) {
             mobileMenu.classList.remove('jz-active');
             mobileMenu.setAttribute('style', 'display: none !important; visibility: hidden !important; opacity: 0 !important; transform: translate3d(-100%, 0, 0);');
          }
          if (mobileOverlay && mobileOverlay.classList.contains('jz-active')) {
             mobileOverlay.classList.remove('jz-active');
             mobileOverlay.setAttribute('style', 'display: none !important; visibility: hidden !important; opacity: 0 !important;');
          }
          document.body.style.overflow = '';
        }
      }, 250);
    });

    // Smooth scroll to anchors with offset - native smooth scroll for desktop and mobile (same as desktop)
    function scrollToAnchor(targetId) {
      const target = document.querySelector(targetId);
      if (!target) {
        console.warn('Target not found:', targetId);
        return;
      }
      
      const header = document.querySelector('.jz-header-section');
      const headerHeight = header ? header.offsetHeight : 80;
      const offset = 80; // Extra offset to show more of the section
      
      // Calculate target position accounting for header
      const targetRect = target.getBoundingClientRect();
      const targetPosition = targetRect.top + window.pageYOffset - headerHeight - offset;
      
      // Show header before scrolling
      if (header) {
        header.classList.remove('jz-header-hidden');
      }
      
      // Native smooth scroll - same for desktop and mobile (exactly as desktop was)
      window.scrollTo({
        top: targetPosition,
        behavior: 'smooth'
      });
    }

    // Handle anchor links - only for desktop nav links, not mobile
    document.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
      const link = e.target.closest('a[href^="#"]');
      if (!link) return;
      
      // Skip if it's a mobile nav link (mobile handles its own scrolling)
      if (link.classList.contains('jz-mobile-nav-link')) {
        return;
      }
      
      const href = link.getAttribute('href');
      if (!href || href === '#') return;
      
      e.preventDefault();
      scrollToAnchor(href);
      
      // Update URL without scrolling
      history.pushState(null, null, href);
    });

      // Scroll Behavior (Hide on scroll down, Show on scroll up)
      let lastScrollY = window.scrollY;
      let isScrollingToAnchor = false;

      window.addEventListener('scroll', () => {
        const currentScrollY = window.scrollY;
        
      // Don't hide if mobile menu is open
      if (document.body.style.overflow === 'hidden') return;

        if (currentScrollY > lastScrollY && currentScrollY > 100) {
          // Scrolling down & past threshold -> Hide
          if (header) header.classList.add('jz-header-hidden');
        } else {
          // Scrolling up or at top -> Show
          if (header) header.classList.remove('jz-header-hidden');
        }

        lastScrollY = currentScrollY;
      }, { passive: true });

    } // End of initNavigation function
    
    // Initialize when DOM is ready
    if (document.readyState === 'loading') {
      document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', initNavigation);
    } else {
      // DOM already loaded
      initNavigation();
    }
    
  })();
</script>

  {% endif %}

  <div class="banner-content {% if section.settings.positioning_mode == 'custom' %}banner-content-custom{% else %}banner-content-{{ section.settings.content_position }}{% endif %}{% if section.settings.animation_style != 'default' %} banner-animation-{{ section.settings.animation_style }}{% endif %}">
    <div class="banner-text-wrapper">
      {% if section.settings.subtitle != blank %}
        <p class="banner-subtitle{% if section.settings.subtitle_bold %} banner-text-bold{% endif %}{% if section.settings.enable_text_shadow %} banner-text-shadow{% endif %}" style="text-align: {{ section.settings.text_alignment }};">{{ section.settings.subtitle }}</p>
      {% endif %}
     
      {% assign lines_count = section.settings.title_lines_count | default: "3" %}
      {% assign logo_pos = section.settings.logo_position | default: "2" %}
      {% assign logo_text_pos = section.settings.logo_text_position | default: "after" %}
     
      {% if section.settings.title_line1 != blank or section.settings.title_line2 != blank or section.settings.title_line3 != blank %}
        <h2 class="banner-title{% if section.settings.title_bold %} banner-text-bold{% endif %}{% if section.settings.enable_text_shadow %} banner-text-shadow{% endif %}" style="align-items: {{ section.settings.text_alignment }};">
          {% if section.settings.title_line1 != blank %}
            <span class="banner-title-line1" style="justify-content: {{ section.settings.text_alignment }};">
              {% if logo_pos == "1" and section.settings.header_logo and logo_text_pos == "before" %}<img src="{{ section.settings.header_logo | img_url: 'master' }}" alt="{{ section.settings.header_logo.alt | escape }}" class="banner-title-logo" width="{{ section.settings.header_logo.width | default: 200 }}" height="{{ section.settings.header_logo.height | default: 50 }}" loading="lazy">{% endif %}{{ section.settings.title_line1 }}{% if logo_pos == "1" and section.settings.header_logo and logo_text_pos == "after" %}<img src="{{ section.settings.header_logo | img_url: 'master' }}" alt="{{ section.settings.header_logo.alt | escape }}" class="banner-title-logo" width="{{ section.settings.header_logo.width | default: 200 }}" height="{{ section.settings.header_logo.height | default: 50 }}" loading="lazy">{% endif %}
            </span>
          {% endif %}
          {% if section.settings.title_line2 != blank %}
            {% if lines_count == "2" or lines_count == "3" %}
              <span class="banner-title-line2" style="justify-content: {{ section.settings.text_alignment }};">
                {% if logo_pos == "2" and section.settings.header_logo and logo_text_pos == "before" %}<img src="{{ section.settings.header_logo | img_url: 'master' }}" alt="{{ section.settings.header_logo.alt | escape }}" class="banner-title-logo" width="{{ section.settings.header_logo.width | default: 200 }}" height="{{ section.settings.header_logo.height | default: 50 }}" loading="lazy">{% endif %}{{ section.settings.title_line2 }}{% if logo_pos == "2" and section.settings.header_logo and logo_text_pos == "after" %}<img src="{{ section.settings.header_logo | img_url: 'master' }}" alt="{{ section.settings.header_logo.alt | escape }}" class="banner-title-logo" width="{{ section.settings.header_logo.width | default: 200 }}" height="{{ section.settings.header_logo.height | default: 50 }}" loading="lazy">{% endif %}
              </span>
            {% endif %}
          {% endif %}
          {% if section.settings.title_line3 != blank %}
            {% if lines_count == "3" %}
              {% assign image_on_line3_pos = section.settings.image_on_line3_position | default: "after" %}
              {% if section.settings.enable_typewriter %}
                {% assign line3_parts = section.settings.title_line3 | split: ' ' %}
                {% assign line3_prefix = '' %}
                {% for part in line3_parts %}
                  {% if forloop.last == false %}
                    {% assign line3_prefix = line3_prefix | append: part | append: ' ' %}
                  {% endif %}
                {% endfor %}
                {% assign line3_first_word = line3_parts | last %}
              {% endif %}
              <span class="banner-title-line3" style="justify-content: {{ section.settings.text_alignment }};">
                {% if logo_pos == "3" and section.settings.header_logo and logo_text_pos == "before" %}<img src="{{ section.settings.header_logo | img_url: 'master' }}" alt="{{ section.settings.header_logo.alt | escape }}" class="banner-title-logo" width="{{ section.settings.header_logo.width | default: 200 }}" height="{{ section.settings.header_logo.height | default: 50 }}" loading="lazy">{% endif %}{% if section.settings.image_on_line3 and image_on_line3_pos == "before" %}<img src="{{ section.settings.image_on_line3 | img_url: 'master' }}" alt="{{ section.settings.image_on_line3.alt | escape }}" class="banner-title-image-line3" width="{{ section.settings.image_on_line3.width | default: 200 }}" height="{{ section.settings.image_on_line3.height | default: 200 }}" loading="lazy">{% endif %}{% if section.settings.enable_typewriter %}{{ line3_prefix }}<span class="typewriter-text" data-words="{{ section.settings.typewriter_words }}" data-speed="{{ section.settings.typewriter_speed }}" data-delay="{{ section.settings.typewriter_delay }}">{{ line3_first_word }}</span><span class="typewriter-cursor">|</span>{% else %}{{ section.settings.title_line3 }}{% endif %}{% if section.settings.image_on_line3 and image_on_line3_pos == "after" %}<img src="{{ section.settings.image_on_line3 | img_url: 'master' }}" alt="{{ section.settings.image_on_line3.alt | escape }}" class="banner-title-image-line3" width="{{ section.settings.image_on_line3.width | default: 200 }}" height="{{ section.settings.image_on_line3.height | default: 200 }}" loading="lazy">{% endif %}{% if logo_pos == "3" and section.settings.header_logo and logo_text_pos == "after" %}<img src="{{ section.settings.header_logo | img_url: 'master' }}" alt="{{ section.settings.header_logo.alt | escape }}" class="banner-title-logo" width="{{ section.settings.header_logo.width | default: 200 }}" height="{{ section.settings.header_logo.height | default: 50 }}" loading="lazy">{% endif %}
                {% if section.settings.image_below_line3 %}
                  <img src="{{ section.settings.image_below_line3 | img_url: 'master' }}"
                       alt="{{ section.settings.image_below_line3.alt | escape }}"
                       class="banner-image-below-line3"
                       width="{{ section.settings.image_below_line3.width | default: 200 }}"
                       height="{{ section.settings.image_below_line3.height | default: 200 }}"
                       loading="lazy">
                {% endif %}
              </span>
            {% endif %}
          {% endif %}
        </h2>
      {% endif %}
     
      {% if section.settings.description != blank %}
        <div class="banner-description{% if section.settings.description_bold %} banner-text-bold{% endif %}{% if section.settings.enable_text_shadow %} banner-text-shadow{% endif %}" style="text-align: {{ section.settings.text_alignment }};">{{ section.settings.description }}</div>
      {% endif %}
     
      <div class="banner-button-wrapper{% if section.settings.button_layout == 'column' %} banner-button-wrapper-column{% endif %}">
        {% if section.settings.button_text != blank %}
          <a href="{{ section.settings.button_link | default: '#' }}"
             class="banner-button banner-button-{{ section.settings.button_style }}{% if section.settings.enable_button_glow %} banner-button-glow{% endif %}{% if section.settings.enable_button_pulse %} banner-button-pulse{% endif %}">
            {{ section.settings.button_text }}
          </a>
        {% endif %}

      </div>
    </div>
  </div>

/* Enhanced Animations */
.banner-content > * {
  animation: fadeInUp 0.8s ease-out forwards;
  opacity: 0;
  transform: translateY(30px);
}

.banner-animation-slide .banner-content > * {
  animation: slideInFromLeft 0.8s ease-out forwards;
}

.banner-animation-zoom .banner-content > * {
  animation: zoomIn 0.8s ease-out forwards;
}

.banner-animation-bounce .banner-content > * {
  animation: bounceIn 0.8s ease-out forwards;
}

.banner-subtitle {
  animation-delay: 0.2s;
}

.banner-title {
  animation-delay: 0.4s;
}

.banner-description {
  animation-delay: 0.6s;
}

.banner-button-wrapper {
  animation-delay: 0.8s;
}

@keyframes fadeInUp {
  to {
    opacity: 1;
    transform: translateY(0);
  }
}

@keyframes slideInFromLeft {
  from {
    opacity: 0;
    transform: translateX(-50px);
  }
  to {
    opacity: 1;
    transform: translateX(0);
  }
}

@keyframes zoomIn {
  from {
    opacity: 0;
    transform: scale(0.5);
  }
  to {
    opacity: 1;
    transform: scale(1);
  }
}

@keyframes bounceIn {
  0% {
    opacity: 0;
    transform: scale(0.3);
  }
  50% {
    opacity: 1;
    transform: scale(1.1);
  }
  100% {
    opacity: 1;
    transform: scale(1);
  }
}
</style>

{% if section.settings.enable_parallax %}
<script>
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
  const bannerSection = document.querySelector('.banner-parallax');
  const bannerImage = bannerSection?.querySelector('.banner-image');
 
  if (bannerSection && bannerImage) {
    function updateParallax() {
      const rect = bannerSection.getBoundingClientRect();
      const windowHeight = window.innerHeight;
     
      if (rect.bottom >= 0 && rect.top <= windowHeight) {
        const scrolled = window.pageYOffset;
        const parallaxOffset = scrolled * 0.5;
        bannerImage.style.transform = `translateY(${parallaxOffset}px)`;
      }
    }
   
    window.addEventListener('scroll', updateParallax);
    updateParallax();
  }
});
</script>
{% endif %}

<script>
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
  {% if section.settings.positioning_mode == 'custom' %}
 
  function forceCustomPositioning() {
    const customContent = document.querySelector('.banner-content-custom');
    if (customContent) {
      customContent.style.position = 'absolute';
      customContent.style.top = '{{ section.settings.content_position_y }}%';
      customContent.style.left = '{{ section.settings.content_position_x }}%';
      customContent.style.transform = 'translate(-50%, -50%)';
      customContent.style.maxWidth = '{{ section.settings.content_max_width }}px';
      customContent.style.zIndex = '999';
      customContent.style.margin = '0';
      customContent.style.padding = '1.5rem';
      customContent.style.width = 'auto';
    }
  }
 
  forceCustomPositioning();
  setTimeout(forceCustomPositioning, 100);
  setTimeout(forceCustomPositioning, 500);
 
  {% endif %}
});
</script>

{% if section.settings.enable_typewriter %}
<script>
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
  const typewriterElement = document.querySelector('.typewriter-text');
  if (!typewriterElement) return;
 
  const wordsStr = typewriterElement.getAttribute('data-words');
  if (!wordsStr) return;
 
  const words = wordsStr.split(',').map(w => w.trim()).filter(w => w.length > 0);
  if (words.length === 0) return;
 
  const speed = parseInt(typewriterElement.getAttribute('data-speed')) || 100;
  const delay = parseInt(typewriterElement.getAttribute('data-delay')) || 2000;
 
  let currentWordIndex = 0;
  let currentCharIndex = words[0].length;
  let isDeleting = false;
  let currentWord = words[0];
  let timeoutId = null;
 
  typewriterElement.textContent = words[0];

  function typeWriter() {
    if (words.length === 0) return;
   
    if (currentWordIndex >= words.length) {
      currentWordIndex = 0;
    }
   
    currentWord = words[currentWordIndex];
   
    if (isDeleting) {
      const deleteSpeed = speed / 2;
      typewriterElement.textContent = currentWord.substring(0, currentCharIndex - 1);
      currentCharIndex--;
     
      if (currentCharIndex < 0) {
        isDeleting = false;
        currentWordIndex++;
        if (currentWordIndex >= words.length) {
          currentWordIndex = 0;
        }
        currentWord = words[currentWordIndex];
        currentCharIndex = 0;
        timeoutId = setTimeout(typeWriter, speed);
        return;
      }
      timeoutId = setTimeout(typeWriter, deleteSpeed);
    } else {
      typewriterElement.textContent = currentWord.substring(0, currentCharIndex + 1);
      currentCharIndex++;
     
      if (currentCharIndex >= currentWord.length) {
        isDeleting = true;
        timeoutId = setTimeout(typeWriter, delay);
        return;
      }
      timeoutId = setTimeout(typeWriter, speed);
    }
  }

  timeoutId = setTimeout(function() {
    isDeleting = true;
    currentCharIndex = words[0].length;
    typeWriter();
  }, delay);

  window.addEventListener('beforeunload', function() {
    if (timeoutId) {
      clearTimeout(timeoutId);
    }
  });
});
</script>
{% endif %}

<script>
  document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
    var buttons = document.querySelectorAll('.banner-button');
    buttons.forEach(function(button) {
      button.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
        var href = this.getAttribute('href');
        if (href && href.startsWith('#')) {
          e.preventDefault();
          var targetId = href.substring(1);
          var targetElement = document.getElementById(targetId);
          if (targetElement) {
            targetElement.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth' });
          }
        }
      });
    });
  });
</script>

@keyframes phoneFadeInUp {
  to {
    opacity: 1;
    transform: translateY(0);
  }
}

@keyframes phoneSlideInFromLeft {
  from {
    opacity: 0;
    transform: translateX(-50px);
  }
  to {
    opacity: 1;
    transform: translateX(0);
  }
}

@keyframes phoneZoomIn {
  from {
    opacity: 0;
    transform: scale(0.5);
  }
  to {
    opacity: 1;
    transform: scale(1);
  }

{% if section.settings.enable_parallax %}
<script>
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
  const bannerSection = document.querySelector('.phone-banner-{{ section.id }}.phone-banner-parallax');
  const bannerImage = bannerSection?.querySelector('.phone-banner-image');
 
  if (bannerSection && bannerImage) {
    function updateParallax() {
      const rect = bannerSection.getBoundingClientRect();
      const windowHeight = window.innerHeight;
     
      if (rect.bottom >= 0 && rect.top <= windowHeight) {
        const scrolled = window.pageYOffset;
        const parallaxOffset = scrolled * 0.5;
        bannerImage.style.transform = `translateY(${parallaxOffset}px)`;
      }
    }
   
    window.addEventListener('scroll', updateParallax);
    updateParallax();
  }
});
</script>
{% endif %}

<script>
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
  {% if section.settings.positioning_mode == 'custom' %}
 
  function forceCustomPositioning() {
    const customContent = document.querySelector('.phone-banner-{{ section.id }} .phone-banner-content-custom');
    if (customContent) {
      customContent.style.position = 'absolute';
      customContent.style.top = '{{ section.settings.content_position_y }}%';
      customContent.style.left = '{{ section.settings.content_position_x }}%';
      customContent.style.transform = 'translate(-50%, -50%)';
      customContent.style.maxWidth = '{{ section.settings.content_max_width }}px';
      customContent.style.zIndex = '999';
      customContent.style.margin = '0';
      customContent.style.padding = '1.5rem';
      customContent.style.width = 'auto';
    }
  }
 
  forceCustomPositioning();
  setTimeout(forceCustomPositioning, 100);
  setTimeout(forceCustomPositioning, 500);
 
  {% endif %}
});
</script>

{% if section.settings.enable_typewriter %}
<script>
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
  const typewriterElement = document.querySelector('.phone-banner-{{ section.id }} .phone-typewriter-text');
  if (!typewriterElement) return;
 
  const wordsStr = typewriterElement.getAttribute('data-words');
  if (!wordsStr) return;
 
  const words = wordsStr.split(',').map(w => w.trim()).filter(w => w.length > 0);
  if (words.length === 0) return;
 
  const speed = parseInt(typewriterElement.getAttribute('data-speed')) || 100;
  const delay = parseInt(typewriterElement.getAttribute('data-delay')) || 2000;
 
  let currentWordIndex = 0;
  let currentCharIndex = words[0].length;
  let isDeleting = false;
  let currentWord = words[0];
  let timeoutId = null;
 
  typewriterElement.textContent = words[0];
 
  function updateImagePosition() {
    const imageBelow = document.querySelector('.phone-banner-{{ section.id }} .phone-banner-image-below-line3');
    if (!imageBelow) return;
   
    const typewriterText = typewriterElement;
    if (!typewriterText) return;
   
    const line3Container = typewriterText.closest('.phone-banner-title-line3');
    if (!line3Container) return;
   
    requestAnimationFrame(function() {
      const textRect = typewriterText.getBoundingClientRect();
      const containerRect = line3Container.getBoundingClientRect();
      const textOffset = textRect.left - containerRect.left;
      const cssOffset = getComputedStyle(imageBelow).getPropertyValue('--image-below-line3-horizontal-offset') || '0px';
      const cssOffsetValue = parseInt(cssOffset) || 0;
      imageBelow.style.left = (textOffset + cssOffsetValue) + 'px';
      imageBelow.style.transform = 'none';
    });
  }
 
  function typeWriter() {
    if (words.length === 0) return;
   
    if (currentWordIndex >= words.length) {
      currentWordIndex = 0;
    }
   
    currentWord = words[currentWordIndex];
   
    if (isDeleting) {
      const deleteSpeed = speed / 2;
      typewriterElement.textContent = currentWord.substring(0, currentCharIndex - 1);
      currentCharIndex--;
     
      if (currentCharIndex < 0) {
        isDeleting = false;
        currentWordIndex++;
        if (currentWordIndex >= words.length) {
          currentWordIndex = 0;
        }
        currentWord = words[currentWordIndex];
        currentCharIndex = 0;
        timeoutId = setTimeout(typeWriter, speed);
        requestAnimationFrame(updateImagePosition);
        return;
      }
      timeoutId = setTimeout(typeWriter, deleteSpeed);
      requestAnimationFrame(updateImagePosition);
    } else {
      typewriterElement.textContent = currentWord.substring(0, currentCharIndex + 1);
      currentCharIndex++;
     
      if (currentCharIndex >= currentWord.length) {
        isDeleting = true;
        timeoutId = setTimeout(typeWriter, delay);
        requestAnimationFrame(updateImagePosition);
        return;
      }
      timeoutId = setTimeout(typeWriter, speed);
      requestAnimationFrame(updateImagePosition);
    }
  }
 
  timeoutId = setTimeout(function() {
    isDeleting = true;
    currentCharIndex = words[0].length;
    typeWriter();
  }, delay);
 
  setTimeout(updateImagePosition, 50);
  setTimeout(updateImagePosition, 200);
  setTimeout(updateImagePosition, 500);
 
  let resizeTimeout;
  window.addEventListener('resize', function() {
    clearTimeout(resizeTimeout);
    resizeTimeout = setTimeout(function() {
      requestAnimationFrame(updateImagePosition);
    }, 100);
  });
 
  window.addEventListener('orientationchange', function() {
    setTimeout(function() {
      requestAnimationFrame(updateImagePosition);
    }, 300);
  });
 
  const observer = new MutationObserver(function() {
    requestAnimationFrame(updateImagePosition);
  });
 
  if (typewriterElement) {
    observer.observe(typewriterElement, {
      childList: true,
      characterData: true,
      subtree: true
    });
  }
 
  window.addEventListener('beforeunload', function() {
    if (timeoutId) {
      clearTimeout(timeoutId);
    }
    if (observer) {
      observer.disconnect();
    }
  });
});
</script>
{% else %}
<script>
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
  function updateImagePosition() {
    const imageBelow = document.querySelector('.phone-banner-{{ section.id }} .phone-banner-image-below-line3');
    if (!imageBelow) return;
   
    const line3Container = imageBelow.closest('.phone-banner-title-line3');
    if (!line3Container) return;
   
    requestAnimationFrame(function() {
      let textElement = null;
      const children = Array.from(line3Container.children);
     
      for (let child of children) {
        if (!child.classList.contains('phone-banner-image-below-line3') &&
            !child.classList.contains('phone-banner-title-logo') &&
            !child.classList.contains('phone-banner-title-image-line3') &&
            child.textContent.trim()) {
          textElement = child;
          break;
        }
      }
     
      if (!textElement) {
        for (let node of line3Container.childNodes) {
          if (node.nodeType === 3 && node.textContent.trim()) {
            const range = document.createRange();
            range.selectNodeContents(node);
            const textRect = range.getBoundingClientRect();
            const containerRect = line3Container.getBoundingClientRect();
            const textOffset = textRect.left - containerRect.left;
           
            const cssOffset = getComputedStyle(imageBelow).getPropertyValue('--image-below-line3-horizontal-offset') || '0px';
            const cssOffsetValue = parseInt(cssOffset) || 0;
            imageBelow.style.left = (textOffset + cssOffsetValue) + 'px';
            imageBelow.style.transform = 'none';
            return;
          }
        }
      }
     
      if (!textElement) {
        const cssOffset = getComputedStyle(imageBelow).getPropertyValue('--image-below-line3-horizontal-offset') || '0px';
        const cssOffsetValue = parseInt(cssOffset) || 0;
        imageBelow.style.left = cssOffsetValue + 'px';
        imageBelow.style.transform = 'none';
        return;
      }
     
      const textRect = textElement.getBoundingClientRect();
      const containerRect = line3Container.getBoundingClientRect();
      const textOffset = textRect.left - containerRect.left;
      const cssOffset = getComputedStyle(imageBelow).getPropertyValue('--image-below-line3-horizontal-offset') || '0px';
      const cssOffsetValue = parseInt(cssOffset) || 0;
      imageBelow.style.left = (textOffset + cssOffsetValue) + 'px';
      imageBelow.style.transform = 'none';
    });
  }
 
  setTimeout(updateImagePosition, 50);
  setTimeout(updateImagePosition, 200);
  setTimeout(updateImagePosition, 500);
 
  let resizeTimeout;
  window.addEventListener('resize', function() {
    clearTimeout(resizeTimeout);
    resizeTimeout = setTimeout(function() {
      requestAnimationFrame(updateImagePosition);
    }, 100);
  });
 
  window.addEventListener('orientationchange', function() {
    setTimeout(function() {
      requestAnimationFrame(updateImagePosition);
    }, 300);
  });
});
</script>
{% endif %}

<script>
document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function() {
  const rows = document.querySelectorAll('.tl-row');

  function update() {
    const trigger = window.innerHeight * 0.65;
    rows.forEach((row, index) => {
      const rect = row.getBoundingClientRect();
      const markerTop = rect.top + 24; 

      if (markerTop < trigger) {
        row.classList.add('active');
      } else {
        row.classList.remove('active');
      }
    });
  }

  window.addEventListener('scroll', update);
  window.addEventListener('resize', update);
  update(); 
});
</script>

  <script>
    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
      // Open/Close Logic
      const contactBtn = document.getElementById('openContactFormBtn');
      const contactOverlay = document.getElementById('contactFormOverlay');
      const closeContact = document.getElementById('closeContactOverlay');

      if(contactBtn && contactOverlay) {
        contactBtn.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
          e.preventDefault();
          contactOverlay.classList.add('active'); // Use existing overlay class logic
          document.body.style.overflow = 'hidden';
        });
      }

      if(closeContact && contactOverlay) {
         closeContact.addEventListener('click', function() {
            contactOverlay.classList.remove('active');
            document.body.style.overflow = '';
         });
      }

      // Close on outside click
      if(contactOverlay) {
        contactOverlay.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
            if (e.target === contactOverlay) {
                contactOverlay.classList.remove('active');
                document.body.style.overflow = '';
            }
        });
      }

      // Form Handling
      const form = document.querySelector('form[action^="/contact"]'); // More robust selector
      const thanks = document.getElementById('thanksMessage');
      
      // Check for success param on load (if page reloaded)
      if (window.location.search.indexOf('contact_posted=true') > -1) {
          // Check if it was the CUSTOM form
          if (sessionStorage.getItem('customFormSubmitted') === 'true') {
             sessionStorage.removeItem('customFormSubmitted');
             
             // Reuse the Contact Overlay but with Custom Text
             if(contactOverlay && thanks) {
                // Set Custom Message
                const titleEl = thanks.querySelector('h3') || thanks.querySelector('h2');
                const pEl = thanks.querySelector('p');
                
                if(titleEl) titleEl.innerText = "Успешно изпратено запитване!";
                if(pEl) pEl.innerHTML = "Благодарим ви! Вашият персонализиран план е получен.<br>Нашият екип ще се свърже с вас в рамките на 24 часа, за да обсъдим детайлите.";
                
                contactOverlay.classList.add('active');
                if(form) form.style.display = 'none';
                thanks.style.display = 'block';
             } else {
                alert("Благодарим ви! Ще се свържем с вас до 24 часа.");
             }
          } else {
              // Standard Contact Form Handling
              if(contactOverlay && thanks && form) {
                  contactOverlay.classList.add('active'); // Re-open modal
                  form.style.display = 'none'; // Hide form
                  thanks.style.display = 'block'; // Show thank you
              }
          }

          // Remove the param from URL to prevent showing it on refresh
          const newUrl = window.location.href.replace('?contact_posted=true', '').replace('&contact_posted=true', '');
          window.history.replaceState({}, document.title, newUrl);
      }

      if(form) {
          // Attempt AJAX submit, but fallback to native if it redirects
          form.addEventListener('submit', function(e) {
            // We'll let it submit natively to ensure Shopify captures it correctly,
            // but we can try to intercept for UX if we are sure it won't redirect.
            // Given the user issues, NATIVE SUBMIT + URL CHECK is safest.
            // So we REMOVE e.preventDefault() to allow reload.
            
            const submitBtn = form.querySelector('.form-submit-btn');
            if(submitBtn) {
                 submitBtn.innerHTML = 'Изпращане...';
                 submitBtn.style.opacity = '0.7';
            }
          });
      }
    });
  </script>

        <!-- Inline Script to populate data -->
        <script>
          function populateHiddenMessage() {
             var paymentVal = customState.paymentType || '-';
             if(typeof getPaymentLabel === 'function') {
                paymentVal = getPaymentLabel(customState.paymentType);
             }
             
             const summary = 
                 "Цел: " + (customState.goal || '-') + "\\n" +
                 "Бранд: " + (customState.brandName || '-') + "\\n" +
                 "Продукти: " + (customState.productType ? customState.productType + ' (' + customState.productCount + ')' : customState.productCount || '-') + "\\n" +
                 "Плащане: " + paymentVal + "\\n" +
                 "Бюджет: " + (customState.budget || '-') + "\\n" +
                 "-------------------\\n" +
                 "Опции: " + (customState.competitors ? customState.competitors : '') + " " + (customState.designAssets ? customState.designAssets : '') + "\\n" +
                 "Ниша: " + (customState.niche || '-') + "\\n" +
                 "Аудитория: " + (customState.audience || '-') + "\\n" +
                 "Визия: " + (customState.vision || '-');
                 
             const el = document.getElementById('hiddenMessage');
             if(el) el.value = summary;
          }
        </script>
      </div>
    </div>
  </div>
