  </style>
  
  <script>
  (function () {
    function initPremiumPricingPackagesSection() {
      const overlay = document.getElementById('interactiveFlow');
      if (!overlay) return;
    
    // Animation Observer
    const observer = new IntersectionObserver((entries) => {
      entries.forEach(entry => {
        if (entry.isIntersecting) {
          entry.target.style.animationPlayState = 'running';
          observer.unobserve(entry.target);
        }
      });
    });
    document.querySelectorAll('.pricing-card').forEach(card => observer.observe(card));
  
    // --- FALLBACK IDs ---
    const FALLBACK_IDS = {
      full: '51974274974043',
      d20: '51861280883035',
      d25: '51861280915803',
      d30: '51861280948571'
    };
  
    // --- FLOW LOGIC ---
    let flowState = {
      planTitle: '',
      fullPrice: 0,
      currency: '',
      vidFull: '', vid20: '', vid25: '', vid30: '',
      goal: '', brandName: '', brandDetails: '', scale: '', paymentType: 'deposit', depositPercent: 20,
      isBooked: false // Track booking status
    };
  
    // Open Flow
    document.querySelectorAll('.start-flow-btn').forEach(btn => {
      btn.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        flowState.planTitle = this.getAttribute('data-plan-title');
        flowState.fullPrice = parseFloat(this.getAttribute('data-plan-price'));
        flowState.currency = this.getAttribute('data-currency');
        
        // Use fallback if attribute is empty or null
        flowState.vidFull = this.getAttribute('data-vid-full') || FALLBACK_IDS.full;
        flowState.vid20 = this.getAttribute('data-vid-20') || FALLBACK_IDS.d20;
        flowState.vid25 = this.getAttribute('data-vid-25') || FALLBACK_IDS.d25;
        flowState.vid30 = this.getAttribute('data-vid-30') || FALLBACK_IDS.d30;
        
        overlay.classList.add('active');
        document.body.classList.add('flow-open');
        resetFlow();
        updatePricesUI();
      });
    });
  
    // Close Flow
    const flowCloseBtn = document.querySelector('.flow-close');
    if (flowCloseBtn) {
      flowCloseBtn.addEventListener('click', () => {
        overlay.classList.remove('active');
        document.body.classList.remove('flow-open');
      });
    }

    const customFlowCloseBtn = document.getElementById('closeCustomFlow');
    if (customFlowCloseBtn) {
      customFlowCloseBtn.addEventListener('click', () => {
        customOverlay.classList.remove('active');
        document.body.classList.remove('flow-open');
      });
    }
  
    // Navigation
    window.nextStep = function(step, value) {
      if (step === 2) flowState.goal = value;
      // Step 3 is Payment, accessed via submitBusinessDetails
      
      document.querySelectorAll('.flow-step').forEach(el => el.classList.remove('active-step'));
      document.getElementById(`step${step}`).classList.add('active-step');
      updateProgressBar(step);
    };

    window.submitBusinessDetails = function() {
      const name = document.getElementById('brandNameInput').value;
      const details = document.getElementById('brandDetailsInput').value;
      
      flowState.brandName = name;
      flowState.brandDetails = details;
      
      nextStep(3); // Go to step 3 (Payment)
    };
  
    window.prevStep = function(step) {
      document.querySelectorAll('.flow-step').forEach(el => el.classList.remove('active-step'));
      document.getElementById(`step${step}`).classList.add('active-step');
      updateProgressBar(step);
    };
  
    function updateProgressBar(step) {
      // Progress bar removed
    }
    
    function resetFlow() {
      document.querySelectorAll('.flow-step').forEach(el => el.classList.remove('active-step'));
      document.getElementById('step1').classList.add('active-step');
      updateProgressBar(1);
      selectPaymentType('deposit');
      flowState.isBooked = false;
      
      // Reset inputs
      const nameInput = document.getElementById('brandNameInput');
      const detailsInput = document.getElementById('brandDetailsInput');
      if (nameInput) nameInput.value = '';
      if (detailsInput) detailsInput.value = '';
      flowState.brandName = '';
      flowState.brandDetails = '';

      const calBtn = document.getElementById('calBookingBtn');
      const calResult = document.getElementById('calBookingResult');
      if (calBtn) calBtn.style.display = 'inline-flex';
      if (calResult) calResult.style.display = 'none';
    }
  
    // Payment Logic
    window.selectPaymentType = function(type) {
      flowState.paymentType = type;
      document.querySelectorAll('.payment-method-card').forEach(el => el.classList.remove('selected-method'));
      
      if (type === 'full') {
        document.getElementById('cardFull').classList.add('selected-method');
      } else {
        document.getElementById('cardDeposit').classList.add('selected-method');
      }
    };
  
    window.selectDeposit = function(percent, event) {
      event.stopPropagation();
      flowState.depositPercent = percent;
      document.querySelectorAll('.deposit-pill').forEach(p => p.classList.remove('selected-pill'));
      event.target.classList.add('selected-pill');
      updatePricesUI();
    };
  
    function updatePricesUI() {
      document.getElementById('displayFullPrice').innerText = flowState.fullPrice;
      
      const priceText = flowState.fullPrice + ' ' + flowState.currency;
      document.getElementById('totalLabelPrice').innerText = priceText;
      
      // Calculate EUR roughly (fixed rate ~1.95583)
      const eurPriceIndex = (flowState.fullPrice / 1.95583).toFixed(2);
      const eurEl = document.getElementById('totalLabelPriceEur');
      if (eurEl) eurEl.innerText = eurPriceIndex + ' €';

      const fullEurEl = document.getElementById('displayFullPriceEur');
      if (fullEurEl) fullEurEl.innerText = eurPriceIndex + ' €';

      document.querySelectorAll('.currency-label').forEach(el => el.innerText = flowState.currency);
      
      const depositVal = Math.round(flowState.fullPrice * (flowState.depositPercent / 100));
      document.getElementById('displayDepositPrice').innerText = depositVal;

      const depositEur = (depositVal / 1.95583).toFixed(2);
      const depEurEl = document.getElementById('displayDepositPriceEur');
      if (depEurEl) depEurEl.innerText = depositEur + ' €';
    }
    
    // --- CAL.COM LISTENER ---
    const cal = window.Cal;
    if(cal) {
      cal("on", {
        action: "bookingSuccessful",
        callback: (e) => {
          // Successful Booking!
          flowState.isBooked = true;
          document.getElementById('calBookingBtn').style.display = 'none';
          document.getElementById('calBookingResult').style.display = 'block';
        }
      });
    }
  
    // Checkout Logic
    const finalCheckoutBtn = document.getElementById('finalCheckoutBtn');
    if (finalCheckoutBtn) finalCheckoutBtn.addEventListener('click', function() {
      let finalVid = '';
      
      // Determine Variant ID
      if (flowState.paymentType === 'full') {
        finalVid = flowState.vidFull;
      } else {
        if (flowState.depositPercent === 20) finalVid = flowState.vid20;
        if (flowState.depositPercent === 25) finalVid = flowState.vid25;
        if (flowState.depositPercent === 30) finalVid = flowState.vid30;
      }
      
      // Fallback Check
      if (!finalVid || finalVid === '') {
         finalVid = FALLBACK_IDS.full; 
      }
      
      // Prepare Data for AJAX
      const formData = {
        'items': [{
          'id': parseInt(finalVid),
          'quantity': 1,
          'properties': {
            'Цел на сайта': flowState.goal,
            'Име на бранда': flowState.brandName || 'Не са посочени',
            'Детайли за бизнеса': flowState.brandDetails || 'Не са посочени',
            'Мащаб': flowState.scale,
            'Тип плащане': flowState.paymentType === 'deposit' ? `Капаро (${flowState.depositPercent}%)` : 'Пълно плащане',
            'Консултация': flowState.isBooked ? '✅ Запазен час (Cal.com)' : 'Без консултация'
          }
        }]
      };
  
      // Button Loading State
      const btn = document.getElementById('finalCheckoutBtn');
      const originalText = btn.innerText;
      btn.innerText = 'Обработка...';
      btn.disabled = true;
  
      // 1. Clear Cart First
      fetch('/cart/clear.js', {
        method: 'POST'
      })
      .then(() => {
          // 2. Add New Item
          return fetch('/cart/add.js', {
            method: 'POST',
            headers: {
              'Content-Type': 'application/json'
            },
            body: JSON.stringify(formData)
          });
      })
      .then(response => {
        if (response.ok) {
          window.location.href = '/checkout';
        } else {
          return response.json().then(errorData => {
             throw new Error(JSON.stringify(errorData));
          });
        }
      })
      .catch(error => {
        console.error('Error:', error);
        alert('Възникна грешка при добавянето в количката.');
        btn.innerText = originalText;
        btn.disabled = false;
      });
    });
  
    // --- CUSTOM FLOW LOGIC ---
    const customOverlay = document.getElementById('customFlow');
    const customList = document.getElementById('customOptionsList');
    const customTotalEl = document.getElementById('customTotalAmount');
    const customCurrencyEl = document.getElementById('customCurrencyLabel');
    
    let customState = {
      options: [],
      selectedIndices: [],
      currency: 'лв.',
      baseVid: '',
      title: '',
      // New fields based on updated questionnaire
      goal: '',
      brandName: '',
      productCount: '',
      competitors: '',
      designAssets: '',
      paymentType: '',
      contentReady: '',
      functionalities: '',
      budget: '',
      isBooked: false,
      productType: '' // New field
    };

    window.setCustomGoal = function(goalValue) {
      customState.goal = goalValue;
      nextCustomStep(2);
    };

    window.nextCustomStep = function(step) {
      try {
        if (step === 2) {
          // Step 1 completed (Goal set via setCustomGoal)
        }
        if (step === 3) {
          // Step 2: Details
          const brandEl = document.getElementById('customBrandName');
          const productEl = document.getElementById('customProductCount');
          const productTypeEl = document.querySelector('input[name="customProductType"]:checked'); // New
          const competitorsEl = document.getElementById('customCompetitors');
          const designEl = document.getElementById('customDesignAssets');
          const visionEl = document.getElementById('customVisionInput');
          const styleEl = document.querySelector('input[name="customStyle"]:checked');

          if(brandEl) customState.brandName = brandEl.value;
          if(productEl) customState.productCount = productEl.value;
          if(productTypeEl) customState.productType = productTypeEl.nextElementSibling.innerText.trim(); // Get label text
          if(competitorsEl) customState.competitors = competitorsEl.value;
          if(designEl) customState.designAssets = designEl.value;
          if(visionEl) customState.vision = visionEl.value;
          if(styleEl) customState.style = styleEl.value;
        }
        if (step === 4) {
          // Step 3: Requirements
          const paymentEl = document.querySelector('input[name="customPaymentType"]:checked');
          const contentEl = document.querySelector('input[name="customContentReady"]:checked');
          const funcEl = document.getElementById('customFunctionalities');
          const budgetEl = document.getElementById('customBudget');

          customState.paymentType = paymentEl ? paymentEl.value : 'Not specified';
          customState.contentReady = contentEl ? contentEl.value : 'Not specified';
          customState.functionalities = funcEl ? funcEl.value : '';
          customState.budget = budgetEl ? budgetEl.value : '';
          
          updateCustomSummary();
        }
        
        const steps = document.querySelectorAll('#customFlow .flow-step');
        if(steps.length > 0) {
          steps.forEach(el => el.classList.remove('active-step'));
          const targetStep = document.getElementById(`customStep${step}`);
          if(targetStep) targetStep.classList.add('active-step');
          
          // SCROLL TO TOP FIX
          const container = document.querySelector('#customFlow .flow-container');
          if(container) container.scrollTop = 0;
          
          updateCustomProgressBar(step);
        }
      } catch (err) {
        console.error("Error in nextCustomStep:", err);
      }
    };

    window.prevCustomStep = function(step) {
      const steps = document.querySelectorAll('#customFlow .flow-step');
      if(steps.length > 0) {
        steps.forEach(el => el.classList.remove('active-step'));
        const targetStep = document.getElementById(`customStep${step}`);
        if(targetStep) targetStep.classList.add('active-step');
        updateCustomProgressBar(step);
      }
    };

    function updateCustomProgressBar(step) {
      // Custom progress bar removed
    }

    function resetCustomFlow() {
      const steps = document.querySelectorAll('#customFlow .flow-step');
      if(steps.length > 0) {
        steps.forEach(el => el.classList.remove('active-step'));
        const step1 = document.getElementById('customStep1');
        if(step1) step1.classList.add('active-step');
      }
      updateCustomProgressBar(1);
      
      // Reset inputs
      const idsToReset = [
        'customBrandName', 'customProductCount', 'customCompetitors', 
        'customDesignAssets', 'customFunctionalities', 'customBudget',
        'customNicheInput', 'customAudienceInput', 'customVisionInput',
        'contactName', 'contactEmail', 'contactPhone', 'contactSocial'
      ];
      
      idsToReset.forEach(id => {
        const el = document.getElementById(id);
        if(el) el.value = '';
      });
      
      customState.isBooked = false;
      
      const calBtn = document.getElementById('customCalBookingBtn');
      const calResult = document.getElementById('customCalBookingResult');
      if (calBtn) calBtn.style.display = 'inline-flex';
      if (calResult) calResult.style.display = 'none';
    }

    function updateCustomSummary() {
      const summaryContent = document.getElementById('customSummaryContent');
      if(!summaryContent) return;

      const total = customTotalEl ? customTotalEl.innerText : '0';

      // 1. Update Visual Summary
      summaryContent.innerHTML = `
        <div class="summary-item"><span class="summary-label">Цел:</span><span class="summary-value">${customState.goal || '—'}</span></div>
        <div class="summary-item"><span class="summary-label">Бранд:</span><span class="summary-value">${customState.brandName || '—'}</span></div>
        <div class="summary-item"><span class="summary-label">Продукти:</span><span class="summary-value">${customState.productType ? customState.productType + ' (' + customState.productCount + ')' : customState.productCount || '—'}</span></div>
        <div class="summary-item"><span class="summary-label">Плащане:</span><span class="summary-value">${getPaymentLabel(customState.paymentType)}</span></div>
        <div class="summary-item"><span class="summary-label">Бюджет:</span><span class="summary-value">${customState.budget || '—'}</span></div>
      `;
      
      // 2. Update Hidden Form Field (Crucial for Email)
      const hiddenMsg = document.getElementById('hiddenMessage');
      if(hiddenMsg) {
          const paymentLabel = (typeof getPaymentLabel === 'function') ? getPaymentLabel(customState.paymentType) : (customState.paymentType || '-');
          hiddenMsg.value = 
             "Цел: " + (customState.goal || '-') + "\n" +
             "Бранд: " + (customState.brandName || '-') + "\n" +
             "Продукти: " + (customState.productType ? customState.productType + ' (' + customState.productCount + ')' : customState.productCount || '-') + "\n" +
             "Плащане: " + paymentLabel + "\n" +
             "Бюджет: " + (customState.budget || '-') + "\n" +
             "-------------------\n" +
             "Опции: " + (customState.competitors ? customState.competitors : '') + " " + (customState.designAssets ? customState.designAssets : '') + "\n" +
             "Ниша: " + (customState.niche || '-') + "\n" +
             "Аудитория: " + (customState.audience || '-') + "\n" +
             "Визия: " + (customState.vision || '-');
      }
    }

    function getPaymentLabel(val) {
      if(!val) return '—';
      if(val === 'Cash on Delivery Only') return 'Само наложен платеж';
      if(val === 'Card Only') return 'С карта';
      if(val === 'Both') return 'И двете';
      if(val === 'No Payments') return 'Няма да има плащания';
      if(val === 'Online Payment') return 'Онлайн'; // Fallback
      if(val === 'Orders Only') return 'Само поръчки'; // Fallback
      return val;
    }
  
    function renderCustomOptions() {
      if(!customList) return;
      customList.innerHTML = '';
      customState.options.forEach((opt, index) => {
        const item = document.createElement('div');
        item.className = 'custom-option-item';
        
        const wrapper = document.createElement('label');
        wrapper.className = 'custom-checkbox-wrapper';
        
        const checkbox = document.createElement('input');
        checkbox.type = 'checkbox';
        checkbox.className = 'custom-option-checkbox';
        checkbox.dataset.index = index;
        checkbox.onchange = (e) => toggleCustomOption(index, e.target.checked);
        
        const name = document.createElement('span');
        name.className = 'custom-option-name';
        name.innerText = opt.name;
        
        wrapper.appendChild(checkbox);
        wrapper.appendChild(name);
        
        const price = document.createElement('div');
        price.className = 'custom-option-price';
        price.innerText = `+${opt.price} ${customState.currency}`;
        
        item.appendChild(wrapper);
        item.appendChild(price);
        
        customList.appendChild(item);
      });
    }
  
    function toggleCustomOption(index, isChecked) {
      if (isChecked) {
        customState.selectedIndices.push(index);
      } else {
        customState.selectedIndices = customState.selectedIndices.filter(i => i !== index);
      }
      updateCustomTotal();
    }
  
    function updateCustomTotal() {
      if(!customTotalEl) return;
      let total = 0;
      customState.selectedIndices.forEach(idx => {
        total += customState.options[idx].price;
      });
      customTotalEl.innerText = total;
    }
  
    // Cal.com for Custom Flow
    if (window.Cal) {
      Cal("on", {
        action: "bookingSuccessful",
        callback: (e) => {
          if (customOverlay && customOverlay.classList.contains('active')) {
            customState.isBooked = true;
            const btn = document.getElementById('customCalBookingBtn');
            const res = document.getElementById('customCalBookingResult');
            if(btn) btn.style.display = 'none';
            if(res) res.style.display = 'block';
          }
        }
      });
    }

    // Open Custom Flow Logic - FIXED
    const startCustomBtns = document.querySelectorAll('.start-custom-flow-btn');
    startCustomBtns.forEach(btn => {
      btn.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        try {
          const rawOptions = this.dataset.options;
          customState.currency = this.dataset.currency;
          customState.baseVid = this.dataset.baseVid;
          customState.title = this.dataset.title;
          customState.selectedIndices = [];
          
          // Parse Options
          if (rawOptions) {
            customState.options = rawOptions.split('\n').map(line => {
              const parts = line.split(':');
              return {
                name: parts[0].trim(),
                price: parts[1] ? parseFloat(parts[1].trim()) : 0
              };
            }).filter(o => o.name);
          } else {
            customState.options = [];
          }
    
          renderCustomOptions();
          updateCustomTotal();
          resetCustomFlow();
          
          if(customOverlay) {
            customOverlay.classList.add('active');
            document.body.classList.add('flow-open');
          } else {
            console.error("Custom overlay not found!");
          }
          
          if(customCurrencyEl) {
            customCurrencyEl.innerText = customState.currency;
          }
        } catch (err) {
          console.error("Error opening custom flow:", err);
        }
      });
    });

    const customCheckoutBtn = document.getElementById('customCheckoutBtn');
    const customSubmitResult = document.getElementById('customSubmitResult');

    // CHECK FOR RETURN from contact submission (custom plan)
    if (window.location.search.indexOf('contact_posted=true') > -1) {
       // Since the URL is shared, we don't know if it came from Normal contact or Custom plan.
       // But we can check if the custom flow was open? No, reload clears JS state.
       // However, the user just wants it to accept. We can show a generic "Thanks" or rely on the standard one.
       // The standard one (lines 310-314) opens 'contactOverlay'. 
       // If we want to show it in the Custom Flow, we'd need a way to persist state.
       // For now, let's assume the standard 'Thanks' modal is sufficient feedback, 
       // OR we can check a sessionStorage flag if we want to re-open the custom flow.
       
       // Let's rely on the native Shopify behavior + the existing success handler I saw earlier.
       // The existing handler opens 'contactOverlay' (the simple contact form). 
       // That might be confusing if they submitted the Custom Plan.
       // Ideally, we'd want to show a specialized success message.
    }

    if (customCheckoutBtn) customCheckoutBtn.addEventListener('click', function() {
      const btn = this;
      const total = customTotalEl ? parseInt(customTotalEl.innerText) : 0;

      const selectedFeatures = customState.selectedIndices.map(idx => {
        const opt = customState.options[idx];
        return `${opt.name} (${opt.price} ${customState.currency})`;
      }).join(', ');

      // Gather contact fields
      const contactName = document.getElementById('contactName').value.trim();
      const contactEmail = document.getElementById('contactEmail').value.trim();
      const contactPhone = document.getElementById('contactPhone').value.trim();
      const contactSocial = document.getElementById('contactSocial').value.trim();

      // Hide any previous result
      if (customSubmitResult) {
        customSubmitResult.style.display = 'none';
      }

      // Validation
      if (!contactName || !contactEmail || !contactPhone) {
        if (customSubmitResult) {
          customSubmitResult.innerHTML = '⚠️ Моля попълнете задължителните полета (Име, Имейл, Телефон).';
          customSubmitResult.style.display = 'block';
          customSubmitResult.style.background = '#fff3cd';
          customSubmitResult.style.color = '#856404';
        }
        return;
      }

      // Email validation
      const emailRegex = /^[^\s@]+@[^\s@]+\.[^\s@]+$/;
      if (!emailRegex.test(contactEmail)) {
        if (customSubmitResult) {
          customSubmitResult.innerHTML = '⚠️ Моля въведете валиден имейл адрес.';
          customSubmitResult.style.display = 'block';
          customSubmitResult.style.background = '#fff3cd';
          customSubmitResult.style.color = '#856404';
        }
        return;
      }

      const bodyMessage = `
Ново запитване за Custom План
=============================

КОНТАКТ:
--------
Име: ${contactName}
Имейл: ${contactEmail}
Телефон: ${contactPhone}
Социална мрежа: ${contactSocial || 'Не е посочено'}

ДЕТАЙЛИ ЗА ПРОЕКТА:
-------------------
Ниша: ${customState.niche || 'Не е посочено'}
Целева аудитория: ${customState.audience || 'Не е посочено'}
Визия: ${customState.vision || 'Не е посочено'}
Стил: ${customState.style || 'Не е посочено'}
Конкуренти: ${customState.competitors || 'Не е посочено'}
Дизайн активи: ${customState.designAssets || 'Не е посочено'}
Тип плащане: ${customState.paymentType || 'Не е посочено'}
Готово съдържание: ${customState.contentReady || 'Не е посочено'}
Функционалности: ${customState.functionalities || 'Не е посочено'}
Бюджет: ${customState.budget || 'Не е посочено'}

ИЗБРАНИ МОДУЛИ:
---------------
${selectedFeatures || 'Няма избрани модули'}

ОБЩА СУМА: ${total} ${customState.currency}
      `;

      // --- REPLACEMENT: USE PRE-RENDERED LIQUID FORM (FIXES CAPTCHA ERROR) ---
      // Instead of creating a form in JS (which lacks CAPTCHA tokens), we use the one we rendered via Liquid.
      
      // --- REPLACEMENT: REUSE THE EXISTING WORKING FORM (Robust Container Select) ---
      
      // We look for the CONTAINER div, not the form directly, because Shopify might change the form's ID.
      const workingFormContainer = document.getElementById('inquiryFormContainer');
      const workingForm = workingFormContainer ? workingFormContainer.querySelector('form') : null;
      
      if(workingForm) {
          // 1. Populate standard fields
          // Note: The Golden Form uses 'input[name="contact[phone]"]' etc.
          const nameInput = workingForm.querySelector('input[name="contact[name]"]');
          const emailInput = workingForm.querySelector('input[name="contact[email]"]');
          const phoneInput = workingForm.querySelector('input[name="contact[phone]"]');
          const socialInput = workingForm.querySelector('input[name="contact[social]"]');
          const typeSelect = workingForm.querySelector('select[name="contact[website_type]"]');
          
          if(nameInput) nameInput.value = contactName;
          if(emailInput) emailInput.value = contactEmail;
          if(phoneInput) phoneInput.value = contactPhone;
          if(socialInput) socialInput.value = contactSocial || 'N/A';
          if(typeSelect && customState.goal) {
             typeSelect.value = customState.goal; 
          }

          // Populate the ID we used in the new "Golden" form: hiddenMessage
          const hiddenBodyInput = workingForm.querySelector('#hiddenMessage');
          if(hiddenBodyInput) hiddenBodyInput.value = bodyMessage; 
          
          btn.innerText = 'Изпращане...';
          btn.disabled = true;

          // 2. DISABLE VALIDATION & FORCE SUBMIT
          workingForm.noValidate = true;
          const requiredInputs = workingForm.querySelectorAll('[required]');
          requiredInputs.forEach(inp => inp.removeAttribute('required'));

          // 3. Submit directly
          workingForm.submit();
          
      } else {
          console.error('Working form container #inquiryFormContainer not found!');
          alert('Възникна системна грешка (Container Not Found). Моля свържете се с нас по телефона.');
      }
    });
  
    // --- COMPARE PLANS LOGIC ---
    const compareOverlay = document.getElementById('compareOverlay');
    const compareDesktop = document.getElementById('compareDesktop');
    const compareMobile = document.getElementById('compareMobile');
    const compareTableBody = document.getElementById('compareTableBody');
    const mobileCompareContent = document.getElementById('mobileCompareContent');
    
    // Open compare overlay
    const compareOpenBtn = document.getElementById('comparePlansBtn');
    if (compareOpenBtn) compareOpenBtn.addEventListener('click', function() {
      compareOverlay.classList.add('active');
      document.body.classList.add('flow-open');
      initializeCompare();
    });
    
    // Close compare overlay
    const compareCloseBtn = document.getElementById('closeCompareOverlay');
    if (compareCloseBtn) compareCloseBtn.addEventListener('click', function() {
      compareOverlay.classList.remove('active');
      document.body.classList.remove('flow-open');
      // Reset mobile state
      const mobileStep1 = document.getElementById('mobileStep1');
      const mobileStep2 = document.getElementById('mobileStep2');
      if (mobileStep1) mobileStep1.style.display = 'block';
      if (mobileStep2) mobileStep2.style.display = 'none';
      document.querySelectorAll('.mobile-plan-option input[type="checkbox"]').forEach(cb => cb.checked = false);
      updateMobileCompareBtn();
    });
    
    // Initialize compare view
    function initializeCompare() {
      const isMobile = window.innerWidth <= 990;
      
      if (isMobile) {
        compareDesktop.style.display = 'none';
        compareMobile.style.display = 'block';
        setupMobileCompare();
      } else {
        compareDesktop.style.display = 'block';
        compareMobile.style.display = 'none';
        setupDesktopCompare();
      }
    }
    
    // --- COMPARISON CONFIG ---
    const COMPARE_CONFIG = [
      { label: 'Продукти', type: 'text', values: ['до 10', 'до 50', 'Неограничен брой'] },
      { label: 'Mobile first', type: 'check', minIndex: 0 },
      { label: 'SEO', type: 'text', values: ['Базово SEO', 'Експертно SEO', 'Експертно SEO'] },
      { label: 'Оптимизация на скоростта', type: 'check', minIndex: 0 },
      { label: 'Генериране на политики', type: 'check', minIndex: 0 },
      { label: 'Проследяване на поръчка', type: 'check', minIndex: 0 },
      { label: 'Upsell, Crossell', type: 'check', minIndex: 1 },
      { label: 'Facebook pixel', type: 'check', minIndex: 1 },
      { label: 'Ревюта', type: 'check', minIndex: 1 },
      { label: 'Имейл маркетинг', type: 'check', minIndex: 1 },
      { label: 'Многоезичност', type: 'check', minIndex: 1 },
      { label: 'Custom функционалности', type: 'check', minIndex: 1 },
      { label: 'Мега меню', type: 'check', minIndex: 1 },
      { label: 'Custom branding', type: 'check', minIndex: 2 },
      { label: 'Мултивалута', type: 'check', minIndex: 2 },
      { label: 'Чат бот', type: 'check', minIndex: 2 },
      { label: '14 дни безплатна поддръжка', type: 'check', minIndex: 2 },
      { label: 'Изпращане на отчети всяка седмица', type: 'check', minIndex: 2 }
    ];

    function getFeatureValue(configItem, planIndex) {
      if (configItem.type === 'text') {
        return configItem.values[planIndex] || '';
      }
      // boolean check
      return planIndex >= configItem.minIndex;
    }

    // Setup desktop compare table
    function setupDesktopCompare() {
      const plans = Array.from(document.querySelectorAll('.pricing-card:not(.custom-plan-card)'));
      const planData = [];

      plans.forEach((card, index) => {
        planData.push({
          index: index,
          title: card.querySelector('.plan-title')?.textContent || '',
          price: card.querySelector('.price-box .amount')?.textContent || '',
          currency: card.querySelector('.price-box .currency')?.textContent || '',
          isPopular: card.classList.contains('popular-card')
        });
      });

      compareTableBody.innerHTML = '';
      
      COMPARE_CONFIG.forEach(item => {
        const row = document.createElement('tr');
        const featureCell = document.createElement('td');
        featureCell.textContent = item.label;
        row.appendChild(featureCell);

        const values = planData.map(plan => getFeatureValue(item, plan.index));
        // Check equality
        const allSame = values.every(v => v === values[0]);

        if (allSame) {
          row.classList.add('same-row');
        } else {
          row.classList.add('diff-row');
        }

        planData.forEach(plan => {
          const cell = document.createElement('td');
          const val = getFeatureValue(item, plan.index);
          
          if (item.type === 'text') {
             cell.innerHTML = `<span style="font-weight:700; color:var(--text-main);">${val}</span>`;
          } else {
             if (val) {
               cell.innerHTML = '<span class="compare-feature-check">✓</span>';
             } else {
               // Use X symbol for false
               cell.innerHTML = '<span class="compare-feature-x" style="color:#ccc; font-weight:bold;">✕</span>';
             }
          }
          row.appendChild(cell);
        });

        compareTableBody.appendChild(row);
      });

      // Initialize state from checkbox (or reset)
      const switchEl = document.getElementById('desktopDiffSwitch');
      if(switchEl) {
         // Reset to 'All' by default when opening
         switchEl.checked = false;
         setDesktopCompareMode('all');
      }
    }

    function setDesktopCompareMode(mode) {
      const switchEl = document.getElementById('desktopDiffSwitch');
      const labelAll = document.getElementById('desktopToggleLabelAll');
      const labelDiff = document.getElementById('desktopToggleLabelDiff');
      const wrapper = document.querySelector('#compareDesktop .compare-table-wrapper');
      
      const isDiff = mode === 'diff';
      
      if (wrapper) {
        // Toggle the class that hides .same-row
        if (isDiff) {
            wrapper.classList.add('diff-only');
        } else {
            wrapper.classList.remove('diff-only');
        }
      }
      
      if (switchEl) switchEl.checked = isDiff;
      if (labelAll) labelAll.classList.toggle('active', !isDiff);
      if (labelDiff) labelDiff.classList.toggle('active', isDiff);
    }
    
    function setMobileCompareMode(mode) {
      const switchEl = document.getElementById('mobileDiffSwitch');
      const labelAll = document.getElementById('mobileToggleLabelAll');
      const labelDiff = document.getElementById('mobileToggleLabelDiff');
      const container = document.getElementById('mobileCompareContent');

      const isDiff = mode === 'diff';

      if (container) {
        container.classList.toggle('diff-only', isDiff);

        // Recalculate alternating colors for visible items
        const allItems = container.querySelectorAll('.mobile-compare-feature-item');

        if (isDiff) {
          // Apply alternating classes only to visible diff items
          let visibleIndex = 0;
          allItems.forEach(item => {
            item.classList.remove('alt-odd', 'alt-even');
            if (item.classList.contains('diff-feature')) {
              if (visibleIndex % 2 === 0) {
                item.classList.add('alt-odd');
              } else {
                item.classList.add('alt-even');
              }
              visibleIndex++;
            }
          });
        } else {
          // Remove all alternating classes in "all" mode
          allItems.forEach(item => {
            item.classList.remove('alt-odd', 'alt-even');
          });
        }
      }

      if (switchEl) switchEl.checked = isDiff;
      if (labelAll) labelAll.classList.toggle('active', !isDiff);
      if (labelDiff) labelDiff.classList.toggle('active', isDiff);
    }

    // Global toggle handler to sync states
    function handleToggleChange(isDiff) {
        setDesktopCompareMode(isDiff ? 'diff' : 'all');
        setMobileCompareMode(isDiff ? 'diff' : 'all');
    }

    if (compareOverlay) {
      compareOverlay.addEventListener('change', (e) => {
         if (e.target.id === 'desktopDiffSwitch' || e.target.id === 'mobileDiffSwitch') {
           handleToggleChange(e.target.checked);
         }
      });
      
      compareOverlay.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
         if (e.target.id === 'desktopToggleLabelAll' || e.target.id === 'mobileToggleLabelAll') {
           handleToggleChange(false);
         }
         if (e.target.id === 'desktopToggleLabelDiff' || e.target.id === 'mobileToggleLabelDiff') {
           handleToggleChange(true);
         }
      });
    }

    function setDesktopCompareMode(mode) {
      const switchEl = document.getElementById('desktopDiffSwitch');
      const labelAll = document.getElementById('desktopToggleLabelAll');
      const labelDiff = document.getElementById('desktopToggleLabelDiff');
      const wrapper = document.querySelector('#compareDesktop .compare-table-wrapper');
      
      const isDiff = mode === 'diff';
      
      if (wrapper) {
        wrapper.classList.toggle('diff-only', isDiff);
      }
      
      if (switchEl) switchEl.checked = isDiff;
      if (labelAll) labelAll.classList.toggle('active', !isDiff);
      if (labelDiff) labelDiff.classList.toggle('active', isDiff);
    }

    // Backwards compatibility (in case something else calls it)
    window.toggleCompareView = function(mode) { setDesktopCompareMode(mode); };
    
    // Setup mobile compare
    function setupMobileCompare() {
      if (compareMobile && compareMobile.dataset.listenersAttached === 'true') {
        return;
      }
      if (compareMobile) {
        compareMobile.dataset.listenersAttached = 'true';
      }
      const checkboxes = document.querySelectorAll('.mobile-plan-option input[type="checkbox"]');
      
      checkboxes.forEach(cb => {
        cb.addEventListener('change', updateMobileCompareBtn);
      });
      
      const mobileCompareBtn = document.getElementById('mobileCompareBtn');
      if (mobileCompareBtn) mobileCompareBtn.addEventListener('click', function() {
        const checked = Array.from(checkboxes).filter(cb => cb.checked);
        if (checked.length === 2) {
          showMobileComparison(checked);
        }
      });
    }
    
    function updateMobileCompareBtn() {
      const checked = document.querySelectorAll('.mobile-plan-option input[type="checkbox"]:checked');
      const btn = document.getElementById('mobileCompareBtn');
      btn.disabled = checked.length !== 2;
    }
    
    function showMobileComparison(checkedBoxes) {
      const plans = checkedBoxes.map(cb => {
        // Get plan index
        const planIndex = parseInt(cb.closest('.mobile-plan-option').dataset.planIndex);
        
        return {
          index: planIndex,
          title: cb.dataset.planTitle,
          price: cb.dataset.planPrice,
          currency: cb.dataset.currency,
          isPopular: cb.dataset.isPopular === 'true',
          description: cb.dataset.description || '',
          vidFull: cb.dataset.vidFull,
          vid20: cb.dataset.vid20,
          vid25: cb.dataset.vid25,
          vid30: cb.dataset.vid30
        };
      });
      
      // Build comparison content
      // Sticky header with ONLY titles
      let html = '<div class="mobile-compare-sticky-header">';
      plans.forEach(plan => {
        html += `<div class="mobile-sticky-title">${plan.title}</div>`;
      });
      html += '</div>';

      // Full plan cards (not sticky)
      html += '<div class="mobile-compare-plans-full">';
      plans.forEach(plan => {
        const showBadge = plan.isPopular;

        html += `
          <div class="mobile-compare-plan-card">

            <div class="mobile-price">
              <span>${plan.currency}</span>
              <span class="mobile-amount">${plan.price}</span>
            </div>
            <p style="font-size: 12px; color: #999; margin: 8px 0 12px 0;">${plan.description}</p>
            <button class="compare-select-btn start-flow-btn"
              data-plan-title="${plan.title}"
              data-plan-price="${plan.price}"
              data-currency="${plan.currency}"
              data-vid-full="${plan.vidFull}"
              data-vid-20="${plan.vid20}"
              data-vid-25="${plan.vid25}"
              data-vid-30="${plan.vid30}">
              Избери
            </button>
          </div>
        `;
      });
      html += '</div>';
      
      // Add features comparison using FIXED CONFIG
      html += '<div class="mobile-compare-row"><h4>Характеристики</h4>';
      
      COMPARE_CONFIG.forEach(item => {
        const val1 = getFeatureValue(item, plans[0].index);
        const val2 = getFeatureValue(item, plans[1].index);
        
        const isSame = val1 === val2;
        const featureClass = isSame ? 'same-feature' : 'diff-feature';
        
        html += `
          <div class="mobile-compare-feature-item ${featureClass}">
            <div class="mobile-feature-name">${item.label}</div>
            <div class="mobile-feature-checks">
        `;
        
        // Render Value 1
        if (item.type === 'text') {
           html += `<span style="font-size:13px; font-weight:700; text-align:center;">${val1}</span>`;
        } else {
           html += `<span class="mobile-check ${val1 ? 'has' : 'no'}">${val1 ? '✓' : '✕'}</span>`;
        }

        // Render Value 2
        if (item.type === 'text') {
           html += `<span style="font-size:13px; font-weight:700; text-align:center;">${val2}</span>`;
        } else {
           html += `<span class="mobile-check ${val2 ? 'has' : 'no'}">${val2 ? '✓' : '✕'}</span>`;
        }

        html += `
            </div>
          </div>
        `;
      });

      html += '</div>';
      
      mobileCompareContent.innerHTML = html;
      
      // Reset switch
      const switchEl = document.getElementById('mobileDiffSwitch');
      if(switchEl) {
        switchEl.checked = false;
        setMobileCompareMode('all');
      }
      
      // Show step 2, hide step 1
      document.getElementById('mobileStep1').style.display = 'none';
      document.getElementById('mobileStep2').style.display = 'block';
      
      // Re-attach event listeners for buttons in comparison
      document.querySelectorAll('#mobileCompareContent .start-flow-btn').forEach(btn => {
        btn.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
          e.preventDefault();
          compareOverlay.classList.remove('active');
          // Trigger the flow
          overlay.classList.add('active');
          flowState.planTitle = this.dataset.planTitle;
          flowState.fullPrice = parseFloat(this.dataset.planPrice);
          flowState.currency = this.dataset.currency;
          flowState.vidFull = this.dataset.vidFull || FALLBACK_IDS.full;
          flowState.vid20 = this.dataset.vid20 || FALLBACK_IDS.d20;
          flowState.vid25 = this.dataset.vid25 || FALLBACK_IDS.d25;
          flowState.vid30 = this.dataset.vid30 || FALLBACK_IDS.d30;
          resetFlow();
          updatePricesUI();
        });
      });
    }
    
    window.mobileBackToStep1 = function() {
      document.getElementById('mobileStep1').style.display = 'block';
      document.getElementById('mobileStep2').style.display = 'none';
      // Reset mobile toggle buttons
      setMobileCompareMode('all');
    };

    function setMobileCompareMode(mode) {
      const switchEl = document.getElementById('mobileDiffSwitch');
      const labelAll = document.getElementById('mobileToggleLabelAll');
      const labelDiff = document.getElementById('mobileToggleLabelDiff');
      const container = document.getElementById('mobileCompareContent');

      const isDiff = mode === 'diff';

      if (container) {
        container.classList.toggle('diff-only', isDiff);

        // Recalculate alternating colors for visible items
        const allItems = container.querySelectorAll('.mobile-compare-feature-item');

        if (isDiff) {
          // Apply alternating classes only to visible diff items
          let visibleIndex = 0;
          allItems.forEach(item => {
            item.classList.remove('alt-odd', 'alt-even');
            if (item.classList.contains('diff-feature')) {
              if (visibleIndex % 2 === 0) {
                item.classList.add('alt-odd');
              } else {
                item.classList.add('alt-even');
              }
              visibleIndex++;
            }
          });
        } else {
          // Remove all alternating classes in "all" mode
          allItems.forEach(item => {
            item.classList.remove('alt-odd', 'alt-even');
          });
        }
      }

      if (switchEl) switchEl.checked = isDiff;
      if (labelAll) labelAll.classList.toggle('active', !isDiff);
      if (labelDiff) labelDiff.classList.toggle('active', isDiff);
    }

    // Backwards compatibility
    window.toggleMobileCompareView = function(mode) { setMobileCompareMode(mode); };
    
    // Handle window resize
    let resizeTimer;
    window.addEventListener('resize', function() {
      clearTimeout(resizeTimer);
      resizeTimer = setTimeout(function() {
        if (compareOverlay.classList.contains('active')) {
          initializeCompare();
        }
      }, 250);
    });

    // Toggle button listeners using Delegation (Robust against DOM replacements)
    if (compareOverlay) {
      // Handle Switch Changes
      compareOverlay.addEventListener('change', (e) => {
         if (e.target.id === 'desktopDiffSwitch') {
           setDesktopCompareMode(e.target.checked ? 'diff' : 'all');
         }
         if (e.target.id === 'mobileDiffSwitch') {
           setMobileCompareMode(e.target.checked ? 'diff' : 'all');
         }
      });
      
      // Handle Label Clicks
      compareOverlay.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
         if (e.target.id === 'desktopToggleLabelAll') setDesktopCompareMode('all');
         if (e.target.id === 'desktopToggleLabelDiff') setDesktopCompareMode('diff');
         if (e.target.id === 'mobileToggleLabelAll') setMobileCompareMode('all');
         if (e.target.id === 'mobileToggleLabelDiff') setMobileCompareMode('diff');
      });
    }
    
    // Re-attach event listeners for compare table buttons
    document.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
      if (e.target.closest('.compare-select-btn')) {
        const btn = e.target.closest('.start-flow-btn');
        if (btn) {
          e.preventDefault();
          compareOverlay.classList.remove('active');
          overlay.classList.add('active');
          // Body stays flow-open since we swap overlays
          flowState.planTitle = btn.dataset.planTitle;
          flowState.fullPrice = parseFloat(btn.dataset.planPrice);
          flowState.currency = btn.dataset.currency;
          flowState.vidFull = btn.dataset.vidFull || FALLBACK_IDS.full;
          flowState.vid20 = btn.dataset.vid20 || FALLBACK_IDS.d20;
          flowState.vid25 = btn.dataset.vid25 || FALLBACK_IDS.d25;
          flowState.vid30 = btn.dataset.vid30 || FALLBACK_IDS.d30;
          resetFlow();
          updatePricesUI();
        }
      }
    });
    }

    if (document.readyState === 'loading') {
      document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', initPremiumPricingPackagesSection);
    } else {
      initPremiumPricingPackagesSection();
    }
    document.addEventListener('shopify:section:load', initPremiumPricingPackagesSection);
  })();
  </script>

  <!-- Contact Success Overlay -->
  <div id="contactFormOverlay" class="flow-overlay" style="align-items: center;">
    <div id="closeContactOverlay" class="flow-close" style="top: 20px; right: 25px;">&times;</div>
    <div class="flow-container" style="max-width: 500px; padding: 40px; text-align: center;">
      <div id="thanksMessage" style="display: block;">
        <div style="font-size: 60px; margin-bottom: 20px;">✅</div>
        <h3 style="font-size: 24px; font-weight: 800; color: #2c3e50; margin-bottom: 15px;">Успешно изпратено!</h3>
        <p style="font-size: 16px; color: #666; line-height: 1.6;">
          Благодарим ви за запитването! Ще се свържем с вас в рамките на 24 часа.
        </p>
        <button class="flow-cta-btn" onclick="document.getElementById('contactFormOverlay').classList.remove('active');" style="margin-top: 25px;">
          Разбрах
        </button>
      </div>
    </div>
  </div>
  
</content>

<script>
  document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function() {
    // Намираме всички видеа с клас .js-ugc-video
    const videos = document.querySelectorAll('.js-ugc-video');

    videos.forEach(video => {
      // Слушаме за събитието 'ended' (когато видеото свърши)
      video.addEventListener('ended', function() {
        // 1. Излизаме от Fullscreen ако е пуснат (за iPhone/Android)
        if (document.exitFullscreen) {
            document.exitFullscreen();
        } else if (document.webkitExitFullscreen) { /* Safari */
            document.webkitExitFullscreen();
        } else if (document.msExitFullscreen) { /* IE11 */
            document.msExitFullscreen();
        }

        // 2. Презареждаме видеото, за да се покаже poster-a
        this.load(); 
      });
    });
  });
</script>

    <script>
      document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function() {
        const projects = document.querySelectorAll('.project-card');
        const btn = document.getElementById('loadMoreBtn');
        
        let visibleCount;
        const initialDesktop = 6;
        const initialMobile = 3;

        function init() {
           if (window.innerWidth > 768) {
             visibleCount = initialDesktop;
           } else {
             visibleCount = initialMobile;
           }
           updateVisibility();
        }

        // Initial setup
        init();
    
        btn.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
          e.preventDefault();
          
          if (window.innerWidth > 768) {
            // Desktop Logic
            if (visibleCount >= projects.length) {
                // Return to initial
                visibleCount = initialDesktop;
                // Optional: Scroll to top of section for better UX
                document.querySelector('.portfolio-section-wrapper').scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth' });
            } else {
                // Show all
                visibleCount = projects.length;
            }
          } else {
            // Mobile Logic
            if (visibleCount >= projects.length) {
                // Return to initial
                visibleCount = initialMobile;
                 document.querySelector('.portfolio-section-wrapper').scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth' });
            } else if (visibleCount === 3) {
                // Show 9
                visibleCount = 9;
            } else {
                // Show All
                visibleCount = projects.length;
            }
          }
          
          updateVisibility();
        });
    
        function updateVisibility() {
          projects.forEach((project, index) => {
            if (index < visibleCount) {
              project.classList.remove('hidden-project');
            } else {
              project.classList.add('hidden-project');
            }
          });
    
          // Update Button Text and Visibility
          if (projects.length <= (window.innerWidth > 768 ? initialDesktop : initialMobile)) {
             // If total projects are less than initial view, hide button
             btn.style.display = 'none';
          } else {
             btn.style.display = 'block';
             if (visibleCount >= projects.length) {
                btn.innerText = "Покажи по-малко";
             } else {
                btn.innerText = "Покажи още";
             }
          }
        }
      });
    </script>

<script>
document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function() {
    // Typewriter Effect
    const words = ["Номер едно", "Топ позиция", "Твоят бизнес"];
    const textElement = document.querySelector(".typing-text");
    let wordIndex = 0;
    let charIndex = 0;
    let isDeleting = false;

    function type() {
        if (!textElement) return;
        const currentWord = words[wordIndex];
        
        if (isDeleting) {
            textElement.textContent = currentWord.substring(0, charIndex - 1);
            charIndex--;
        } else {
            textElement.textContent = currentWord.substring(0, charIndex + 1);
            charIndex++;
        }

        if (!isDeleting && charIndex === currentWord.length) {
            isDeleting = true;
            setTimeout(type, 1500); // Pause at end
        } else if (isDeleting && charIndex === 0) {
            isDeleting = false;
            wordIndex = (wordIndex + 1) % words.length;
            setTimeout(type, 500); // Pause before new word
        } else {
            setTimeout(type, isDeleting ? 50 : 100);
        }
    }
    type();
});
</script>

<script>
document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function() {
  const section = document.querySelector('.full-reveal-section');
  const mover = document.querySelector('.chat-content-mover');
  const viewport = document.querySelector('.chat-viewport');
  const messages = document.querySelectorAll('.msg-row');
  const sbTime = document.querySelector('.sb-time');
  const timestamp = document.querySelector('.timestamp');

  function updateTime() {
    const now = new Date();
    let hours = now.getHours();
    let minutes = now.getMinutes();
    const ampm = hours >= 12 ? 'PM' : 'AM';
    const hours12 = hours % 12 || 12;
    const minutesStr = minutes < 10 ? '0' + minutes : minutes;
    const strTime = `${hours12}:${minutesStr}`;
    if (sbTime) sbTime.textContent = strTime;
    if (timestamp) timestamp.textContent = `Today ${strTime} ${ampm}`;
  }

  setInterval(updateTime, 1000);
  updateTime();

  if (!section || !mover || !viewport) return;

  const lerp = (start, end, factor) => start + (end - start) * factor;
  let currentTranslateY = 0;
  let targetTranslateY = 0;

  function animate() {
    currentTranslateY = lerp(currentTranslateY, targetTranslateY, 0.1);
    mover.style.transform = `translate3d(0, -${currentTranslateY}px, 0)`;
    requestAnimationFrame(animate);
  }
  animate();

  window.addEventListener('scroll', () => {
    const rect = section.getBoundingClientRect();
    const sectionH = section.offsetHeight;
    const windowH = window.innerHeight;

    if (rect.top <= windowH && rect.bottom >= 0) {
      let rawProgress = (windowH - rect.top) / (sectionH + windowH);
      const startBuffer = 0.15;
      const endBuffer = 0.85;
      let activePhysicalProgress = (rawProgress - startBuffer) / (endBuffer - startBuffer);

      if (activePhysicalProgress < 0) activePhysicalProgress = 0;
      if (activePhysicalProgress > 1) activePhysicalProgress = 1;

      const activeProgress = activePhysicalProgress;
      const totalMessages = messages.length;
      const messagesToShow = Math.floor(activeProgress * (totalMessages + 2));

      messages.forEach((msg, index) => {
        if (index < messagesToShow) msg.classList.add('visible');
      });

      let contentHeight = 0;
      if (messagesToShow > 0 && messagesToShow <= totalMessages) {
        const lastMsg = messages[messagesToShow - 1];
        contentHeight = lastMsg.offsetTop + lastMsg.offsetHeight;
      } else if (messagesToShow > totalMessages) {
        contentHeight = mover.scrollHeight;
      }

      const viewportHeight = viewport.offsetHeight;
      if (contentHeight > (viewportHeight - 60)) {
        targetTranslateY = contentHeight - viewportHeight + 40;
      } else {
        targetTranslateY = 0;
      }
    }
  }, { passive: false });
});
</script>
